            "lse AS is_nullable,",
            "    CAST(pg_get_expr(ad.adbin, ad.adrelid) AS varchar) AS column_default,",

            "         WHEN 23 \/*int4*\/ THEN 32",
            "         WHEN 20 \/*int8*\/ THEN 64",

            "               ELSE ((atttypmod - 4) >> 16) & 65535",

            "    CAST(pg_get_expr(ad.adbin, ad.adrelid) AS varchar) AS column_default,",
            "    coalesce(pg_get_expr(ad.adbin, ad.adrelid) ~ 'nextval',false) AS is_autoinc,",

            "         WHEN 23 \/*int4*\/ THEN 32",

            "         ELSE null",
            "      END   AS numeric_precision,",
            "      CASE",

            "        END",
            "           ELSE null",
            "      END AS numeric_scale,",
            "    CAST(",

{
    "datatext": {
        "SELECT\n    d.nspname AS table_schema,\n    c.relname AS table_name,\n    a.attname AS column_name,\n    t.typname AS data_type,\n    a.attlen AS character_maximum_length,\n    pg_catalog.col_description(c.oid, a.attnum) AS column_comment,\n    a.atttypmod AS modifier,\n    a.attnotnull ": [
            "lse AS is_nullable,",
            "    CAST(pg_get_expr(ad.adbin, ad.adrelid) AS varchar) AS column_default,",
            "    coalesce(pg_get_expr(ad.adbin, ad.adrelid) ~ 'nextval',false) AS is_autoinc,",
            "    array_to_string((select array_agg(enumlabel) from pg_enum where enumtypid=a.atttypid)::varchar[],',') as enum_values,",
            "    CASE atttypid",
            "         WHEN 21 \/*int2*\/ THEN 16",
            "         WHEN 23 \/*int4*\/ THEN 32",
            "         WHEN 20 \/*int8*\/ THEN 64",
            "         WHEN 1700 \/*numeric*\/ THEN",
            "              CASE WHEN atttypmod = -1",
            "               THEN null",
            "               ELSE ((atttypmod - 4) >> 16) & 65535",
            "               END",
            "         WHEN 700 \/*float4*\/ THEN 24 \/*FLT_MANT_DIG*\/",
            "         WHEN 701 \/*float8*\/ THEN 53 \/*DBL_MANT_DIG*\/",
            "         ELSE null",
            "      END   AS numeric_precision,",
            "      CASE",
            "        WHEN atttypid IN (21, 23, 20) THEN 0",
            "        WHEN atttypid IN (1700) THEN",
            "        CASE",
            "            WHEN atttypmod = -1 THEN null",
            "            ELSE (atttypmod - 4) & 65535",
            "        END",
            "           ELSE null",
            "      END AS numeric_scale,",
            "    CAST(",
            "             information_schema._pg_char_max_length(information_schema._pg_truetypid(a, t), information_schema._pg_truetypmod(a, t))",
            "             AS numeric",
            "    ) AS size,",
            "    a.attnum = any (ct.conkey) as is_pkey",
            "FROM",
            "    pg_class c",
            "    LEFT JOIN pg_attribute a ON a.attrelid = c.oid",
            "    LEFT JOIN pg_attrdef ad ON a.attrelid = ad.adrelid AND a.attnum = ad.adnum",
            "    LEFT JOIN pg_type t ON a.atttypid = t.oid",

            "lse AS is_nullable,",
            "    CAST(pg_get_expr(ad.adbin, ad.adrelid) AS varchar) AS column_default,",
            "    coalesce(pg_get_expr(ad.adbin, ad.adrelid) ~ 'nextval',false) AS is_autoinc,",
            "    array_to_string((select array_agg(enumlabel) from pg_enum where enumtypid=a.atttypid)::varchar[],',') as enum_values,",
            "    CASE atttypid",
            "         WHEN 21 \/*int2*\/ THEN 16",
            "         WHEN 23 \/*int4*\/ THEN 32",
            "         WHEN 20 \/*int8*\/ THEN 64",
            "         WHEN 1700 \/*numeric*\/ THEN",
            "              CASE WHEN atttypmod = -1",
            "               THEN null",
            "               ELSE ((atttypmod - 4) >> 16) & 65535",
            "               END",
            "         WHEN 700 \/*float4*\/ THEN 24 \/*FLT_MANT_DIG*\/",
            "         WHEN 701 \/*float8*\/ THEN 53 \/*DBL_MANT_DIG*\/",
            "         ELSE null",
            "      END   AS numeric_precision,",
            "      CASE",
            "        WHEN atttypid IN (21, 23, 20) THEN 0",
            "        WHEN atttypid IN (1700) THEN",
            "        CASE",
            "            WHEN atttypmod = -1 THEN null",
            "            ELSE (atttypmod - 4) & 65535",
            "        END",
            "           ELSE null",
            "      END AS numeric_scale,",
            "    CAST(",
            "             information_schema._pg_char_max_length(information_schema._pg_truetypid(a, t), information_schema._pg_truetypmod(a, t))",
            "             AS numeric",
            "    ) AS size,",
            "    a.attnum = any (ct.conkey) as is_pkey",
            "FROM",
            "    pg_class c",
            "    LEFT JOIN pg_attribute a ON a.attrelid = c.oid",
            "    LEFT JOIN pg_attrdef ad ON a.attrelid = ad.adrelid AND a.attnum = ad.adnum",
            "    LEFT JOIN pg_type t ON a.atttypid = t.oid",
            "    LEFT JOIN pg_namespace d ON d.oid = c.relnamespace",
            "    LEFT join pg_constraint ct on ct.conrelid=c.oid and ct.contype='p'",

            "    a.attnum > 0 and t.typname != ''",
            "    and c.relname = 'clientes'",
            "    and d.nspname = 'public'",
            "ORDER BY",
            "    a.attnu"

            "lse AS is_nullable,",
            "    CAST(pg_get_expr(ad.adbin, ad.adrelid) AS varchar) AS column_default,",
            "    coalesce(pg_get_expr(ad.adbin, ad.adrelid) ~ 'nextval',false) AS is_autoinc,",
            "    array_to_string((select array_agg(enumlabel) from pg_enum where enumtypid=a.atttypid)::varchar[],',') as enum_values,",
            "    CASE atttypid",
            "         WHEN 21 \/*int2*\/ THEN 16",
            "         WHEN 23 \/*int4*\/ THEN 32",
            "         WHEN 20 \/*int8*\/ THEN 64",
            "         WHEN 1700 \/*numeric*\/ THEN",
            "              CASE WHEN atttypmod = -1",
            "               THEN null",
            "               ELSE ((atttypmod - 4) >> 16) & 65535",
            "               END",
            "         WHEN 700 \/*float4*\/ THEN 24 \/*FLT_MANT_DIG*\/",
            "         WHEN 701 \/*float8*\/ THEN 53 \/*DBL_MANT_DIG*\/",
            "         ELSE null",
            "      END   AS numeric_precision,",
            "      CASE",
            "        WHEN atttypid IN (21, 23, 20) THEN 0",
            "        WHEN atttypid IN (1700) THEN",
            "        CASE",
            "            WHEN atttypmod = -1 THEN null",
            "            ELSE (atttypmod - 4) & 65535",
            "        END",
            "           ELSE null",
            "      END AS numeric_scale,",
            "    CAST(",
            "             information_schema._pg_char_max_length(information_schema._pg_truetypid(a, t), information_schema._pg_truetypmod(a, t))",
            "             AS numeric",
            "    ) AS size,",
            "    a.attnum = any (ct.conkey) as is_pkey",
            "FROM",
            "    pg_class c",
            "    LEFT JOIN pg_attribute a ON a.attrelid = c.oid",
            "    LEFT JOIN pg_attrdef ad ON a.attrelid = ad.adrelid AND a.attnum = ad.adnum",
            "    LEFT JOIN pg_type t ON a.atttypid = t.oid",

            "lse AS is_nullable,",
            "    CAST(pg_get_expr(ad.adbin, ad.adrelid) AS varchar) AS column_default,",
            "    coalesce(pg_get_expr(ad.adbin, ad.adrelid) ~ 'nextval',false) AS is_autoinc,",
            "    array_to_string((select array_agg(enumlabel) from pg_enum where enumtypid=a.atttypid)::varchar[],',') as enum_values,",
            "    CASE atttypid",
            "         WHEN 21 \/*int2*\/ THEN 16",
            "         WHEN 23 \/*int4*\/ THEN 32",
            "         WHEN 20 \/*int8*\/ THEN 64",
            "         WHEN 1700 \/*numeric*\/ THEN",
            "              CASE WHEN atttypmod = -1",
            "               THEN null",
            "               ELSE ((atttypmod - 4) >> 16) & 65535",
            "               END",
            "         WHEN 700 \/*float4*\/ THEN 24 \/*FLT_MANT_DIG*\/",
            "         WHEN 701 \/*float8*\/ THEN 53 \/*DBL_MANT_DIG*\/",
            "         ELSE null",
            "      END   AS numeric_precision,",
            "      CASE",
            "        WHEN atttypid IN (21, 23, 20) THEN 0",
            "        WHEN atttypid IN (1700) THEN",
            "        CASE",
            "            WHEN atttypmod = -1 THEN null",
            "            ELSE (atttypmod - 4) & 65535",
            "        END",
            "           ELSE null",
            "      END AS numeric_scale,",
            "    CAST(",
            "             information_schema._pg_char_max_length(information_schema._pg_truetypid(a, t), information_schema._pg_truetypmod(a, t))",
            "             AS numeric",
            "    ) AS size,",
            "    a.attnum = any (ct.conkey) as is_pkey",
            "FROM",
            "    pg_class c",
            "    LEFT JOIN pg_attribute a ON a.attrelid = c.oid",
            "    LEFT JOIN pg_attrdef ad ON a.attrelid = ad.adrelid AND a.attnum = ad.adnum",
            "    LEFT JOIN pg_type t ON a.atttypid = t.oid",
